('Liam', '4.0 out of 5 stars', "\nI usually never write reviews but seeing this mug has such a good reputation I feel like you should know some details about it.I had one that I used for a year and a half and it was leaking sometimes. I could just figure it out why when I got the new one.The little piece that is supposed to lock the whole mechanism in place and provide the seal has a groove that it needs to go in when you rotate it a little. The lip of the groove is so weak that it just scraps itself of with each assembly. You can see the damage and I just got this thermos today. It has just happend after disassambling and reassembling three times. For comparison last picture shows how it looks on my old lid.When the lip is gone the small piece that holds the whole mechanism together can easily rotste and slide out over time, especially when it is hot and moist(i.e. when you have coffee in it) . It happened to me it can happen to you too.I consider the locking mechanism grinding itself off a major design problem.I like the feel of this cup a lot actually. It is the one that I don't accidently burn my mouth when drinking.
